Manage Spring POJO Life Cycle 
         Programmetic
         Declarative
         Annotation


- Its container responsibility to manage the life cycle of the bean.
- How ?

		A.  Programmetic
         	B.  Declarative
                C.  Annotation


# spring container
	
           controler           service         dao  
             init()             init()          init()

             //                 //             //

             destroy()         destroy()         destroy()

             

#Manage Spring POJO Life Cycle - Programmetic

          s-1  create  maven java project
          s-2  include all the spring dependency
          s-3  add  spring.xml
          s-4  create Bean class  Test.java
          s-4  add  client.java 
         


#Test.java

class Test implements InitializingBean, DisposableBean {

    private String username;
    private String password;
    private String driverName;
    private String urlName;


    @Override
    public void afterPropertiesSet() throws Exception {

        System.out.println("init called");

    }

    public void insertDb(){
        System.out.println("Database insert");
    }

    @Override
    public void destroy() throws Exception {
        System.out.println("destroy called");
    }


    public Test(String username, String password, String driverName, String urlName) {
        this.username = username;
        this.password = password;
        this.driverName = driverName;
        this.urlName = urlName;
    }

    public Test() {
    }

    public String getUsername() {
        return username;
    }

    public void setUsername(String username) {
        this.username = username;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Test{" +
                "username='" + username + '\'' +
                ", password='" + password + '\'' +
                ", driverName='" + driverName + '\'' +
                ", urlName='" + urlName + '\'' +
                '}';
    }

    public void setPassword(String password) {
        this.password = password;
    }

    public void setDriverName(String driverName) {
        this.driverName = driverName;
    }

    public void setUrlName(String urlName) {
        this.urlName = urlName;
    }

    public String getPassword() {
        return password;
    }

    public String getDriverName() {
        return driverName;
    }

    public String getUrlName() {
        return urlName;
    }
}


#spring.xml

<!DOCTYPE beans PUBLIC "-//SPRING//DTD BEAN 2.0//EN"
        "https://www.springframework.org/dtd/spring-beans-2.0.dtd">
<beans>
        <bean id="obj"  class="org.example.Test">
            <property name="driverName" value="oracle.jdbc.driver.JdbcDriver"/>
            <property name="urlName" value="jdbc:oracle:thin:1521:xe"/>
            <property name="username" value="system"/>
            <property name="password" value="oracle"/>
        </bean>
</beans>




#Manage Spring POJO Life Cycle - Declarative

          s-1  create  maven java project
          s-2  include all the spring dependency
          s-3  add  spring.xml
          s-4  create Bean class  Test.java
          s-4  add  client.java 


- bean class should not implement - InitializingBean, DisposableBean
- create your userdefined init() and destroy()
- define init-method="initdemo" destroy-method="destroydemo" as an attribute of bean element inside pom.xml



#Test.java

class Test {

    private String username;
    private String password;
    private String driverName;
    private String urlName;


    public  void initdemo(){
          System.out.println("init called");
    }


    public void insertDb(){
        System.out.println("Database insert");
    }

    public void destroydemo(){
        System.out.println("destroy called");
    }


    public Test(String username, String password, String driverName, String urlName) {
        this.username = username;
        this.password = password;
        this.driverName = driverName;
        this.urlName = urlName;
    }

    public Test() {
    }

    public String getUsername() {
        return username;
    }

    public void setUsername(String username) {
        this.username = username;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Test{" +
                "username='" + username + '\'' +
                ", password='" + password + '\'' +
                ", driverName='" + driverName + '\'' +
                ", urlName='" + urlName + '\'' +
                '}';
    }

    public void setPassword(String password) {
        this.password = password;
    }

    public void setDriverName(String driverName) {
        this.driverName = driverName;
    }

    public void setUrlName(String urlName) {
        this.urlName = urlName;
    }

    public String getPassword() {
        return password;
    }

    public String getDriverName() {
        return driverName;
    }

    public String getUrlName() {
        return urlName;
    }
}



#spring.xmnl
<!DOCTYPE beans PUBLIC "-//SPRING//DTD BEAN 2.0//EN"
        "https://www.springframework.org/dtd/spring-beans-2.0.dtd">
<beans>
        <bean id="obj"  class="org.example.Test" init-method="initdemo" destroy-method="destroydemo">
            <property name="driverName" value="oracle.jdbc.driver.JdbcDriver"/>
            <property name="urlName" value="jdbc:oracle:thin:1521:xe"/>
            <property name="username" value="system"/>
            <property name="password" value="oracle"/>
        </bean>
</beans>

        <bean id="obj"  class="org.example.Test" >
            <property name="driverName" value="oracle.jdbc.driver.JdbcDriver"/>
            <property name="urlName" value="jdbc:oracle:thin:1521:xe"/>
            <property name="username" value="system"/>
            <property name="password" value="oracle"/>
        </bean>

#Test.java
class Test {

    private String username;
    private String password;
    private String driverName;
    private String urlName;


    @PostConstruct
    public  void initdemo(){
          System.out.println("init called");
    }


    public void insertDb(){
        System.out.println("Database insert");
    }

    @PreDestroy
    public void destroydemo(){
        System.out.println("destroy called");
    }


    public Test(String username, String password, String driverName, String urlName) {
        this.username = username;
        this.password = password;
        this.driverName = driverName;
        this.urlName = urlName;
    }

    public Test() {
    }

    public String getUsername() {
        return username;
    }

    public void setUsername(String username) {
        this.username = username;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Test{" +
                "username='" + username + '\'' +
                ", password='" + password + '\'' +
                ", driverName='" + driverName + '\'' +
                ", urlName='" + urlName + '\'' +
                '}';
    }

    public void setPassword(String password) {
        this.password = password;
    }

    public void setDriverName(String driverName) {
        this.driverName = driverName;
    }

    public void setUrlName(String urlName) {
        this.urlName = urlName;
    }

    public String getPassword() {
        return password;
    }

    public String getDriverName() {
        return driverName;
    }

    public String getUrlName() {
        return urlName;
    }
}

                                                                   - Bean class should implement 2 interface  ie  InitializationBean,DisposableBeans

                                                                                 3.  Create  spring.xml
                                                                                 4.   Create  EmpDb.java
                                                                                 5.   create client.java

     
                                                                    class     EmpDb  implements InitializationBean,DisposableBean{

                                                                               private String driver;
                                                                               private String url;
                                                                               private String userid;
                                                                               private String pass;
                                                                                 Connection con =null

                                                                               afterPropertiesSet(){
                                                                                             class.forName("");
                                                                                             con= DriverManager.getConnection("","","")
                                                                                              System.out.println("connection success")
                                                                               }

                                                                                public void insert(){
                                                                                                 System.out.println("Data inserted")                  
                                                                                  
                                                                                }

                                                                                destroy(){
                                                                                                con.close()
					System.out.println("connection closed")
                                                                                }
			            }

#Secondary Type Injection:
- container can inject one class object inside another class.
      - ref inside spring.xml
      - engine instance variable inside Car.java
      - we have to provide getters and setters inside car class.

class  Car{

          Engine engine;

          //getters and setters 


}

class  Engine{



}

#Autowire

             Controller            Service               DAO           DB
              POJO                  POJO                 POJO


 <bean id="c1"  class="Controller">
    <property name="service" ref="s1">
 </bean>

  <bean id="s1"  class="Service">
     <property name="dao" ref="d1">
 </bean>

 <bean id="d1"  class="Dao">

 </bean>


@Autowired

       - not required getters and setters of one class instance inside another class.
       - not required constructor of one class instance inside another class.
       - not required ref





class   Controller {


   @Autowired
   Service service;


}

class  Service{


    @Autowired
    DAO  dao;


}

class  DAO{



}

Spring MVC 
     1. Spring MVC  work above Spring IOC container.
     2. Spring MVC follow front controller design pattern in the presentation tier.
     3. Spring MVC follow  Data Access Object pattern in the integration tier.
     


#MVC  using Servlet : limitation

#MVC  Using JSP : limitation

# J2EE Design Pattern

- Front Controller:
-	As application grow , number of servlet grow to handle the client request.
-	We have to implement Authentication , Authorization and manage view for each servlet.
-	Solution : Centralized Request Handling mechanism.
-	Front Controller will do automatically authentication/authorization/logging and then 
-       Pass the request to the corresponding handler User.


-Data Access Object :
	-It is used to separate low level data access API from high level business service.
                    -Data access from persistence storage.
	-Manipulation of Data.
                    -Decouple persistence storage from your application.


# Spring MVC Life cycle :

  s-1  first request will come to front controller is DispatcherServlet.
  s-2  DispatcherServlet forward the request to Handler Servlet  like LoginController.java
  s-3  LoginController will return  the login status to the DispatcherServlet in the format of String or ModelAndView Object.
  s-4  DispatcherServlet  will take help of ViewResolver to identify the response status from HandlerController.
  s-5  Once DispatcherServlet find the response status from ViewResolver , send the same response to the client.

Usecase:  Login

	
		view        		  controller       		 service   	     dao       db

                LoginView.jsp             LoginController.java
    

#Spring MVC project Using Maven(intellij)

Hands On Demo : Spring MVC Login Application

 1. Create maven project using webapp dependency


 2. Add spring mvc  and servlet dependency


<dependency>
  <groupId>org.springframework</groupId>
  <artifactId>spring-webmvc</artifactId>
  <version>4.3.3.RELEASE</version>
</dependency>

<dependency>
  <groupId>javax.servlet</groupId>
  <artifactId>servlet-api</artifactId>
  <version>2.5</version>
  <scope>provided</scope>
</dependency>

 3. Create index.jsp  , success.jsp , failure.jsp , LoginPage.jsp inside jsp folder.


//index.jsp
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<meta charset="ISO-8859-1">
<title>Insert title here</title>
</head>
<body>

       Welcome  to  Spring MVC

       <a href="/login2">login</a>

</body>
</html>


//LoginPage.jsp
<html>
<head>
<title>Insert title here</title>
</head>
<body>
<form method="post" action="/Login">
		UserId : <input type="text" name="userId" /></br>
		UserName : <input type="text" name="userName" /></br>
		<input type="submit" value="Submit" />
	</form>
</body>
</html>



4. Create web.xml file.


<!DOCTYPE web-app PUBLIC
        "-//Sun Microsystems, Inc.//DTD Web Application 2.3//EN"
        "http://java.sun.com/dtd/web-app_2_3.dtd" >
<web-app>
  <welcome-file-list>
    <welcome-file>/WEB-INF/jsp/index.jsp</welcome-file>
  </welcome-file-list>

  <servlet>
    <servlet-name>spring-dispatcher</servlet-name>
    <servlet-class>org.springframework.web.servlet.DispatcherServlet</servlet-class>
    <init-param>
      <param-name>contextConfigLocation</param-name>
      <param-value>/WEB-INF/config/spring-dispatcher-servlet.xml</param-value>
    </init-param>
  </servlet>
  <servlet-mapping>
    <servlet-name>spring-dispatcher</servlet-name>
    <url-pattern>/</url-pattern>
  </servlet-mapping>
</web-app>


6. Create spring-dispatcher-servlet.xml inside config directory.



<beans  xmlns="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans"
        xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"
        xmlns:aop="http://www.springframework.org/schema/aop"
        xmlns:context="http://www.springframework.org/schema/context"
        xmlns:jee="http://www.springframework.org/schema/jee"
        xmlns:lang="http://www.springframework.org/schema/lang"
        xmlns:p="http://www.springframework.org/schema/p"
        xmlns:tx="http://www.springframework.org/schema/tx"
        xmlns:util="http://www.springframework.org/schema/util"
        xmlns:mvc="http://www.springframework.org/schema/mvc"
        xsi:schemaLocation="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans/spring-beans.xsd
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/aop http://www.springframework.org/schema/aop/spring-aop.xsd
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/context http://www.springframework.org/schema/context/spring-context.xsd
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/jee http://www.springframework.org/schema/jee/spring-jee.xsd
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/lang http://www.springframework.org/schema/lang/spring-lang.xsd
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/tx http://www.springframework.org/schema/tx/spring-tx.xsd
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/util http://www.springframework.org/schema/util/spring-util.xsd>
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/mvc http://www.springframework.org/schema/mvc/spring-mvc-3.1.xsd">


    <context:component-scan  base-package="com"/>

    <mvc:annotation-driven/>

    <bean id="viewResolver"
          class="org.springframework.web.servlet.view.InternalResourceViewResolver">
        <property name="prefix">
            <value>WEB-INF/jsp/</value>
        </property>
        <property name="suffix">
            <value>.jsp</value>
        </property>
    </bean>


</beans>







7. create controller component


@Controller("loginController")
public class LoginController {

    @RequestMapping(value = "/login2", method = RequestMethod.GET)
    public ModelAndView loginPageView() {
        ModelAndView obj = new ModelAndView("LoginPage");
        return obj;
    }

    @RequestMapping(value="/Login", method=RequestMethod.POST)
    public ModelAndView loginCheck(HttpServletRequest request) {

        String  userid = request.getParameter("userId");
        String  pass = request.getParameter("pass");

        if(userid.equals("ABC")) {
            ModelAndView  obj=new ModelAndView("success");
            return obj;
        }
        ModelAndView  fobj=new ModelAndView("failure");
        return fobj;
    }

}

//SpringBoot RAD Features

			1. auto-configuration

      @SpringBootApplication = @Configuration +@EnableAutoConfiguration +@ComponentScan

			@Component - to find all the classes in the classpath
			@ComponentScan  - enable @Component Scan
			@EnableAutoConfiguration - auto configuration scan the class path , 
					find a library  in the class path then attempt to 
					guess the best configuration for the existing app.


			2. embedded server
			


			3. Bootstrap the application
				- It enable scaning of the config classes
				files , and load them into SpringContext.

			4. starter spring-boot template 
				spring-boot-starter - web
				spring-boot-starter- test
				spring-boot-starter- jersey
				spring-boot-starter- aop
				spring-boot-starter- hateoas
				spring-boot-starter- security

@Controller
public class LoginController {
	
	
	@GetMapping("/home")
	public ModelAndView loginpageview() {
		return new ModelAndView("LoginPage");
	}
	
	
	@PostMapping("/login")
	public ModelAndView loginCheck(HttpServletRequest request) {
		
		String userId = request.getParameter("userId");
		String pass = request.getParameter("pass");
		
	     
		
		if(userId.equals("ABC")
			return new ModelAndView("success");
		else
			return new ModelAndView("failure");
			
	}
}

Web Service
            #Distributed Environment Communication
            - RMI - support homogeneous communication not heterohgeneous 
	    - CORBA - support homogeneous communication and heterohgeneous  - implementation cost is high
            - web service - support homogeneous communication and heterohgeneous
            - using web service we expose the function as vendor independent format.
            - 2 type of web service 
			A. SOAP Based
				- xml based 
                                - xml,xslt,xsd,xpath,xquery,...

			B. REST Based WS
                                - Json based

	
Spring DAO    

          - DAO will communicate with Databse using Spring Data JPA
          - Spring DAO:
		Spring JDBC
		Spring Data JPA
          - Spring Data JPA use Hibernate , Eclipse link as JPA Provider
          - Hibernate , Eclipse link providing ORM

ORM 
	- Class name should map Table name
        - class instance var should map column name
        - object should map table row.

WHY  ORM ?
        -  we can make our application Database independent.

ORM:                            using ORM
      Java Class(Restaurant) ----------------> Table


        @Entity
        Restaurant ----------------------> TableName

        @Id
	restId  ------------------------> ColumnName
     




c. Create Entity

@Entity
public class Restaurant  {

    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    @Column(name="rest_id")
    private Long restId;

    private String name;

    private String email;

    @Column(name="mobile_number")
    private String mobileNumber;

	//getters setters and constructor

}


- check if entity table created in the table.





				mins - 5 mins












D. create repository

- create package repository
- we should define repository as interface 
- we should use the CRUD method provided by SpringBoot spec




@Repository
public interface RestaurantRepository extends JpaRepository<Restaurant, Long> {

    Optional<Restaurant> findByMobileNumber(String name);

}
















E. create service and serviceimpl


public interface IRestService {

    void createRest(Restaurant restaurant);
    Restaurant fetchRest(String mobileNumber);
    boolean updateRest(Restaurant restaurant);
    boolean deleteRest(String mobileNumber);
}




@Service
public class IRestServiceImpl implements IRestService{

    @Autowired
    RestRepository restaurantRepository;


    @Override
    public void createRest(Restaurant restaurant) {
        restaurantRepository.save(restaurant);
    }


    public Restaurant fetchRestaurant(String mobileNumber) {
        return restaurantRepository.findByMobileNumber(mobileNumber).orElseThrow(
                () -> new ResourceNotFoundException("Restaurant", "mobileNumber", mobileNumber)
        );
    }


    @Override
    public Restaurant fetchRest(String mobileNumber) {
        return null;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean updateRest(Restaurant restaurant) {
        return false;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean deleteRest(String mobileNumber) {
        return false;
    }
}



F. Create Controller


@org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController
@RequestMapping("/api")
@AllArgsConstructor
public class RestController {

    @Autowired
    IRestServiceImpl irestServiceImpl;

    @PostMapping("/create")
    public ResponseEntity<Restaurant> createRestaurant(@RequestBody Restaurant restaurant){
            irestServiceImpl.createRest(restaurant);
            return (ResponseEntity<Restaurant>) ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CREATED).body(restaurant);
    }

    @GetMapping("/fetch")
    public ResponseEntity<Restaurant> fetchRestaurantDetails(@RequestParam
                                                                String mobileNumber) {
        Restaurant restaurant = irestServiceImpl.fetchRestaurant(mobileNumber);
        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.OK).body(restaurant);
    }

}

@Repository
public interface RestRepository extends CrudRepository<Restaurant,Long> {

#service

@Service
public class RestServiceImpl implements RestService {

	
	@Autowired
	RestRepository  restRepository;
	
	public void createRest(Restaurant restaurant) {
		
		restRepository.save(restaurant);
	}

	@Override
	public Restaurant fetchRestaurant(String mobileNumber) {
		
		return restRepository.findByMobileNumber(mobileNumber).orElseThrow(
				()-> new ResourceNotFoundException("Restaurant","mobileNumber",mobileNumber)
		);	
	}
}


#Exception

@ResponseStatus(value = HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND)
public class ResourceNotFoundException extends RuntimeException {

	public ResourceNotFoundException(String resourceName, String fieldName, String fieldValue) {
   	super(String.format("%s not found with the given input data %s : '%s'", resourceName, fieldName, fieldValue));

}
}





#controller

@RequestMapping("/api")
@org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController
public class RestController {
	
	@Autowired
	RestServiceImpl    restServiceImpl;
	
	@PostMapping("/create")
    public ResponseEntity<Restaurant> createRestaurant(@RequestBody Restaurant restaurant){
		
		    restServiceImpl.createRest(restaurant);
            
            return (ResponseEntity<Restaurant>) ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CREATED).body(restaurant);
    }

	
	@GetMapping("/fetch")
    public ResponseEntity<Restaurant> fetchRestaurant(@RequestParam String mobileNumber){
		
			Restaurant  restaurant = restServiceImpl.fetchRestaurant(mobileNumber);
		
            return (ResponseEntity<Restaurant>) ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.OK).body(restaurant);
    }

	
}

#Buzz words About MS


1. Size: Micro service follow fine grained approached based web service.


                                fine grained 
		class Employee{    =================================>   web service

			m1()

			m2()

		}
	
                                coarse grained 
		class Employee{   ==================================>  web service

			m1()

			m2()

			m3()

			m4()

			m5()

		}

2.  Distributed - Using micro service one server can communicate with other server.


3.  DDD -

4.  Autonomy

5.  REST is not the only way   rpc ,grpc , severless

<%@ taglib uri="http://java.sun.com/jsp/jstl/core" prefix="c"%>
<html>
<head>
    <title>Student CRUD (REST + JSP)</title>
    <script src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-3.6.0.min.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
<h2>Student Management</h2>

<form id="studentForm">
    <input type="hidden" id="id" />
    Name: <input type="text" id="name"/><br/>
    Email: <input type="text" id="email"/><br/>
    Course: <input type="text" id="course"/><br/>
    <button type="submit">Save</button>
</form>

<hr/>

<table border="1" id="studentTable">
    <thead>
        <tr>
            <th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>Email</th><th>Course</th><th>Actions</th>
        </tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody></tbody>
</table>

<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
    loadStudents();

    // Load all students
    function loadStudents(){
        $.get("/api/students", function(data){
            let rows = "";
            data.forEach(s => {
                rows += "<tr>" +
                    "<td>"+s.id+"</td>" +
                    "<td>"+s.name+"</td>" +
                    "<td>"+s.email+"</td>" +
                    "<td>"+s.course+"</td>" +
                    "<td>" +
                        "<button onclick='editStudent("+JSON.stringify(s)+")'>Edit</button>" +
                        "<button onclick='deleteStudent("+s.id+")'>Delete</button>" +
                    "</td>" +
                "</tr>";
            });
            $("#studentTable tbody").html(rows);
        });
    }

    // Save (Create/Update)
    $("#studentForm").submit(function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        let id = $("#id").val();
        let student = {
            name: $("#name").val(),
            email: $("#email").val(),
            course: $("#course").val()
        };

        if(id){ // update
            $.ajax({
                url: "/api/students/"+id,
                type: "PUT",
                contentType: "application/json",
                data: JSON.stringify(student),
                success: function(){ loadStudents(); resetForm(); }
            });
        } else { // create
            $.ajax({
                url: "/api/students",
                type: "POST",
                contentType: "application/json",
                data: JSON.stringify(student),
                success: function(){ loadStudents(); resetForm(); }
            });
        }
    });
});

// Edit Student
function editStudent(s){
    $("#id").val(s.id);
    $("#name").val(s.name);
    $("#email").val(s.email);
    $("#course").val(s.course);
}

// Delete Student
function deleteStudent(id){
    if(confirm("Are you sure?")){
        $.ajax({
            url: "/api/students/"+id,
            type: "DELETE",
            success: function(){ location.reload(); }
        });
    }
}

// Reset form
function resetForm(){
    $("#id").val("");
    $("#name").val("");
    $("#email").val("");
    $("#course").val("");
}
</script>

</body>
</html>

#conroller

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/students")
public class StudentRestController {

    private final StudentRepository repo;

    public StudentRestController(StudentRepository repo) {
        this.repo = repo;
    }

    @GetMapping
    public List<Student> getAll() {
        return repo.findAll();
    }

    @GetMapping("/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity<Student> getById(@PathVariable Long id) {
        return repo.findById(id).map(ResponseEntity::ok)
                .orElse(ResponseEntity.notFound().build());
    }

    @PostMapping
    public Student create(@RequestBody Student student) {
        return repo.save(student);
    }

    @PutMapping("/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity<Student> update(@PathVariable Long id, @RequestBody Student student) {
        return repo.findById(id).map(s -> {
            s.setName(student.getName());
            s.setEmail(student.getEmail());
            s.setCourse(student.getCourse());
            return ResponseEntity.ok(repo.save(s));
        }).orElse(ResponseEntity.notFound().build());
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity<Object> delete(@PathVariable Long id) {
        return repo.findById(id).map(s -> {
            repo.delete(s);
            return ResponseEntity.noContent().build();
        }).orElse(ResponseEntity.notFound().build());
    }
}




@Service
public class StudentService {

    private final StudentRepository repo;

    public StudentService(StudentRepository repo) {
        this.repo = repo;
    }

    public List<Student> listAll() {
        return repo.findAll();
    }

    public Student save(Student student) {
        return repo.save(student);
    }

    public Student get(Long id) {
        return repo.findById(id).orElseThrow();
    }

    public void delete(Long id) {
        repo.deleteById(id);
    }
}


public interface StudentRepository extends JpaRepository<Student, Long> {
}




package com.example.springbootlogin.entity;

import jakarta.persistence.Entity;
import jakarta.persistence.GeneratedValue;
import jakarta.persistence.GenerationType;
import jakarta.persistence.Id;

@Entity
public class Student {

    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    private Long id;

    private String name;
    private String email;
    private String course;

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student{" +
                "id=" + id +
                ", name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", email='" + email + '\'' +
                ", course='" + course + '\'' +
                '}';
    }

    public Long getId() {
        return id;
    }

    public void setId(Long id) {
        this.id = id;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public String getEmail() {
        return email;
    }

    public void setEmail(String email) {
        this.email = email;
    }

    public String getCourse() {
        return course;
    }

    public void setCourse(String course) {
        this.course = course;
    }

    public Student() {
    }

    public Student(Long id, String name, String email, String course) {
        this.id = id;
        this.name = name;
        this.email = email;
        this.course = course;
    }
}

#index.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html xmlns:th="http://www.thymeleaf.org">
<head>
    <title>Students</title>
</head>
<body>
<h2>Student List</h2>
<a th:href="@{/new}">Add New</a>
<table border="1">
    <tr>
        <th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>Email</th><th>Course</th><th>Actions</th>
    </tr>
    <tr th:each="student : ${students}">
        <td th:text="${student.id}"></td>
        <td th:text="${student.name}"></td>
        <td th:text="${student.email}"></td>
        <td th:text="${student.course}"></td>
        <td>
            <a th:href="@{'/edit/' + ${student.id}}">Edit</a>
            <a th:href="@{'/delete/' + ${student.id}}"
               onclick="return confirm('Are you sure?')">Delete</a>
        </td>
    </tr>
</table>
</body>
</html>



#form.html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html xmlns:th="http://www.thymeleaf.org">
<head>
    <title>Student Form</title>
</head>
<body>
<h2 th:text="${student.id == null ? 'Add Student' : 'Edit Student'}"></h2>
<form th:action="@{/save}" th:object="${student}" method="post">
    <input type="hidden" th:field="*{id}"/>
    Name: <input type="text" th:field="*{name}" required/><br/>
    Email: <input type="email" th:field="*{email}" required/><br/>
    Course: <input type="text" th:field="*{course}" required/><br/>
    <button type="submit">Save</button>
</form>
<a th:href="@{/}">Back</a>
</body>
</html>

#StudentViewController.java

@Controller
public class StudentViewController {

    private final StudentService service;

    public StudentViewController(StudentService service) {
        this.service = service;
    }

    @GetMapping("/")
    public String index(Model model) {
        model.addAttribute("students", service.listAll());
        return "index";
    }

    @GetMapping("/new")
    public String newForm(Model model) {
        model.addAttribute("student", new Student());
        return "form";
    }

    @PostMapping("/save")
    public String save(@ModelAttribute("student") Student student) {
        service.save(student);
        return "redirect:/";
    }

    @GetMapping("/edit/{id}")
    public String editForm(@PathVariable Long id, Model model) {
        model.addAttribute("student", service.get(id));
        return "form";
    }

    @GetMapping("/delete/{id}")
    public String delete(@PathVariable Long id) {
        service.delete(id);
        return "redirect:/";
    }
}




@Entity
public class Student {

    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    private Long id;

    private String name;
    private String email;
    private String course;

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student{" +
                "id=" + id +
                ", name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", email='" + email + '\'' +
                ", course='" + course + '\'' +
                '}';
    }

    public Long getId() {
        return id;
    }

    public void setId(Long id) {
        this.id = id;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public String getEmail() {
        return email;
    }

    public void setEmail(String email) {
        this.email = email;
    }

    public String getCourse() {
        return course;
    }

    public void setCourse(String course) {
        this.course = course;
    }

    public Student() {
    }

    public Student(Long id, String name, String email, String course) {
        this.id = id;
        this.name = name;
        this.email = email;
        this.course = course;
    }
}



public interface StudentRepository extends JpaRepository<Student, Long> {
}




package com.example.springbootlogin.service;

import com.example.springbootlogin.entity.Student;
import com.example.springbootlogin.repository.StudentRepository;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import java.util.List;

@Service
public class StudentService {

    private final StudentRepository repo;

    public StudentService(StudentRepository repo) {
        this.repo = repo;
    }

    public List<Student> listAll() {
        return repo.findAll();
    }

    public Student save(Student student) {
        return repo.save(student);
    }

    public Student get(Long id) {
        return repo.findById(id).orElseThrow();
    }

    public void delete(Long id) {
        repo.deleteById(id);
    }
}

		//Python Data Types and Variable:


                                      java-  byte , short , int , long , float , double , boolean , char
                                              -  primitive types


                                     python 

		    - all data type in python is object.
                                                   - type() define the datatype of each object.
                                                   - each object uniquely identified by a number.   id()
                                                   - object inside pvm allocate resource from heap.
                                                   - Any object inside python - two types


                                                                         a.  mutable object (list , dict , set .....)
                                                                                            - once created can be changed


                                                                         b.  immutable object  (int , float , string ,frozent set,....)
                                                                                           - once created can not be changed
                                                                                           str = "hello"
                                                                                           str = "hello"+"world"
                                                                                           print(str)

		//Control Flow  Using Python
			A program's control flow is the order in which the program's code executes.
			1.  selection statement  (if else switch)
                                                            2.  iterative statement  (for , while , do while)
                                   
                                    //selection statement 
                                    class       SelectionControlDemo:
                                    	       def   method1(self):
                                             	x  =  7
                                                        y  =  6
                                                        if  x < y :
                                                              print("x less than y")
                                                        elif x > y:
                                                              print("x greater than y")
                                                        elif  x == y:
                                                              print("x equals to y")
                                                        else:
                                                              print("none of the above")

                                     obj =  SelectionControlDemo()
                                     obj.method1()




                                      // iterative statement 

                                          java
                                               for(int i =0 ; i < 10 ; i++)
                                                           System.out.println(i); 

                                                for (int   i  :  arr)
                                                            System.out.println(i)

                                           python
                                             
                                                 for  x  in  range(0,10):
			print(x)

                                                 for  y  in  "This is a social media app":
			print(y)

                                                  array = ["abc","xyz","pqr","ddd"]
                                                  for  b  in array:
                                                             print(b)

                                                   a = 2
                                                   b= 20
                                                   while  a < b :
			print("a is less than b")
